The nose behind this fragrance is Yann Vasnier. Top notes are Pink Pepper, Pear, Indonesian Nutmeg, elemi and Bergamot; middle notes are Rose, Clove, Magnolia and Flax; base notes are Cashmeran, Haitian Vetiver, Sandalwood, Sylkolide and Amber. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>Toy Boy, the first fragrance for men designed by creative director Jeremy Scott, follows the Toy line, launched by the first unisex edition in 2014 and followed by Toy 2 for women from 2018.</p>

<p>"Toy Boy is the new exclusive fragrance by Moschino that reinterprets elegance with a touch of irony. It speaks to a unique, dynamic, enthusiastic and passionate man, but one who is not afraid to reveal his more tender and playful side. Toy Boy is an exciting play of endless codes seeking out re-evaluation and liberation."</p>

<p>Top notes: Italian bergamot, green pear, elemi, pink pepper, Indonesian nutmeg<br />
Heart: magnolia, rose asbolute, clove bud, flex flower<br />
Base: Haitian vetiver orpour, cashmerean, sandalwood, ambermax, sylkolide (musk)</p>

<p>The legendary Moschino bear is lacquered in an opaque black in the bottle of the new fragrance. The face of the perfume is Brazilian model Jhona Burjack, shot by photographer Giampaolo Sgura.</p>

<p>Moschino Toy Boy is available as a 30, 50 and 100 ml Eau de Parfum, acconmanied by grooming line. <br />

To be completely fair, I think I would have substituted the nutmeg and/or clove (to me, this is what gives it the very, 'mature,' feel) for something else (oak moss, birch?) but I can live with it. Niche smelling, gives modern pansexual hippie vibes... hope it doesn’t get discontinued.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="2343896"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=2343896#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2338435" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2338435" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Pharagonescia"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2164380"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2164380.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Pharagonescia" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2338435ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2338435" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.71); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2164380">Pharagonescia</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-11-04">11/04/24 22:02</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>It is written that Alexander the Great himself exuded a beautiful floral aroma. Alexander also worshipped the rose, spread the flowers throughout the lands he conquered, acquired many new cultivars from distant places, and some speculate the rose was the center piece of the Vergina Sun Star that came to symbolize Alexander and his Macedonian roots.<br />
<br />
Toy Boy is a rose and salted pear duo, mineralic, sweaty, clean. Upon the very first moment I smelled Toy Boy I knew there was something pheromonal and shockingly reminiscent of floral and intoxicating pits advertising histocompatibility, luring prospective mates. Seduction by love potion.<br />
<br />
There is an entirely different animalic category that perfumery has never quite confronted and certainly not sufficiently explored: that of the delicious, naughty, and intoxicating replications of floral and ripe fruity odorants produced by humans at the peak of their reproductive cycle. The aroma of bodies in heat. These molecules have ancient evolutionary roots and truly mystical powers to draw a lover close, to bond mates for a lifetime, or to repel the incompatible from each other's presence. Magic chemistry and deep natural wisdom. <br />
<br />
Whether by chance or skill, Yan Vasnier has discovered something other perfumers have not. It is only fitting that as one of the few - or maybe the first - fragrance to capture male virility in such an accurately floral and fruity manner, Toy Boy lures with the promise of a rose. Rose is after all the fragrance of ancient beauty and conquest. So very Alexandrian.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="2338435"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=2338435#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2335065" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2335065" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Decisional"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1339380"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1339380.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Decisional" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Yves-Saint-Laurent/L-Homme-Eau-de-Parfum-72727.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.72727.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="L'Homme Eau de Parfum"title="L'Homme Eau de Parfum"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2335065ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2335065" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.8); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1339380">Decisional</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-11-01">11/01/24 18:39</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Got this as a gift from a friend, had had it on my want list for a while based SOLELY on the amazingness of the bottle, little did I know that the scent of this thing would also be downright amazing.<br />
<br />
In the same way I described the colour sensation of wearing Eau de Gaga as deep electric purple there is something undeniably crimson red about this. It's not a BLOOD smell or anything vampiristic like that, but there is such a deep, DEEP red rose here, the most "masculine" and HEAVY rose I've ever smelled, combined with a very fresh leather. The fruit freshness ascribed to pear in the notes I'm not sure if I'm able to single out myself, but it is while heavy on rose and leather still somehow a fresh scent to wear, one that WILL lift your spirits, and I thoroughly enjoyed sniffing myself constantly wearing this, and I would for a long time since it's quite a performance beast, and ESPECIALLY at its amazing price.<br />
<br />
Quite the compliment-getter as well, I cannot recommend this enough to a man sure enough of himself to wear a rose scent, or a woman who wants a leather smell that doesn't lean too harsh. Basically a perfume for anyone of any gender who dares to be a bit non-conformist. I love it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="2335065"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=2335065#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2331349" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1823504">Electriclady</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-27">10/27/24 09:24</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is my first ever Moschino fragrance. I have been looking for a replacement for Stella McCartney which has sadly long since been discontinued. I love rose, and was intrigued about this one given that it gets good reviews.<br />
While sadly it isn't going to take the place of my beloved Stella, it is absolutely beautiful. I'm sorry I originally overlooked this one because I found the bottle quite tacky. I get Moschino's playful design but wonder if that means people like me don't take them seriously.<br />
It's a spicy, woody earthy rose with a juicy and watery air. Not as intense as The Different Company's Rose Poivree mind you, which I also love, but I really do like it. And despite the awfully tacky bottle, would consider buying it again.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="2329220"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=2329220#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2327171" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It’s a very strong dirty rose (and by that i mean it’s a realistic rose with its dirt and stem) scent — the pink pepper is extra spicy, and the rest of the notes are here to make the perfume more complex, as they don’t have much presence. <br />
This is a niche fragrance. Yeah. Quite a challenging one, in fact, and I could only bring me to appreciate it in a cold night. This one’s for clubbing, ok? It’s very seductive and very sexual, just like the ads for it. I love the bear aesthetic (i think it’s contradictory in a cool way), but i must warn y’all: if you’re a more gourmand person, do know this is NOT for you; Hell, i think this isn’t even for anyone who isn’t prepared. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1648729"><a href="/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection" class="__cf_email__" data-cfemail="9fc8f2feeda9a9a8acdff8f2fef6f3b1fcf0f2">[email&#160;protected]</a></b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-22">10/22/24 09:58</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Tom Ford’s Black Orchid had a kid, he grew up and went to college, but he loved to party, skipped classes, suffered from ADD, and talked incessantly about Top Gun…his name was Toy Boy. This fragrance is the strongest scent I own. The sheen on your hand lasts for hours. It’s a very unique concoction; it opens with a herbaceous green peppercorn zing that is slowly enveloped by a huge sweet floral cloud that kind of mutes the spicey vetiver and nutmeg, but they pop out from time to time and it’s fantastic when they do. There is also a little bit of animalic bite way down deep. A very simple way to describe this is AF’s Fierce covered in a fine mist of sweet and soft rose…it’s more complicated than that but you will pick up the fierce DNA later in the dry down. I really like Toy Boy, but it’s so strong and bratty that I rarely wear it out and about, and instead, save for around the house when I want to smell something interesting. If you enjoy unique and interesting frags you will love this one. If you’re looking for a signature scent sample first.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="2323843"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=2323843#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2318879" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
Another update, a few days later. I love this scent. It's got a pickle/cucumber fresh scent with a sugary touch. Just amazing, unique. Already a favorite. Hoping it stays that way - if a cologne never gets old, that puts it with the best.<br />
<br />
Update #4. I cant stop smellign this stuff. I want to drink it. I'll be wearing this one in my regular rotation for a long time.<br />

Couple days more - one of my favorite colognes. This is such a unique scent that I can't get over, the rose and pepper is a blend that just punches a hole through all the conventions of perfumery and leaves you with a fragrance that is a niche diamond.<br />
If PdM were to copy this and call it Rosalia, you'd see it gatekept to hell and back.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="2289186"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=2289186#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2289097" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2289097" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="oceansoflorewi"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1225449"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1225449.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="oceansoflorewi" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Dolce-Gabbana-pour-Homme-1994-483.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.483.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Dolce&Gabbana pour Homme (1994)"title="Dolce&Gabbana pour Homme (1994)"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2289097ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2289097" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1225449">oceansoflorewi</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-20">09/20/24 05:53</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The revolutionary 'Le Male' of the 2020's - despite if the public has responded to it.<br />
<br />
(Me previous to Toy Boy):<br />
For the love of god. Please someone shelf this baked sickening vanilla trend but still give me a playful polarizing one of a kind DNA for men that stops strangers dead in their tracks to ask what outer dimensional DNA I am wearing (What Le Male did for the 90s when dominant vanilla wasn't a man's note). <br />
<br />
Moschino listened to these pleas and made a brilliant playful rich Rose fragrance for men - so beastly it has 68% VOL - 32% Oils. To make it even more masterful- the perfumer didn't just take a generic unisex DNA and marketed it for men- it really does have a masculine forward aroma and darker facets to it. Its gotten decent hype - but I'm sincerely surprised this hasn't made a bigger presence in the 5 years its been out - I never smell this anywhere but my own arm. <br />
<br />
The closest I could compare this to in terms of its style is Y EDP - Playful rich crowd pleasing EDP without dominant sickening sweet base notes (A dying and or neglected fragrance style). Compared to YEDP though - Toy Boy has no tonka, no vanilla nothing! And smells nothing in terms of the actual DNA of Y EDP- this Toy Boy is one of a kind. I HATE sweet scents - even on a date I'd rather wear something in the likes of DG The one edp. <br />
<br />
I really don't get why women have convinced us to smell like cupcakes - go ahead and buy this to smell like Fruity spicy rose petals and ambery woods.<br />
<br />
M A S T E R P I E C E</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="2289097"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=2289097#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2288642" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1739093">chuckt808</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-10">09/10/24 11:51</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>As others have noted, this could be a niche frag at 5 times the price, which is wild.  Opens with a lot of rose, pink pepper, pear, and elemi.  Some more florals come through briefly and then dries down to pink pepper and vetiver with some rose and nutmeg from the opening still lingering.  This is pretty much a cross between Isfarkand (pink pepper, citrus, vetiver) and Nawab of Oudh Intensivo (rose, magnolia, citrus, vetiver and a general greenness) by Ormonde Jayne.  Maybe not quite as deep as Nawab but certainly better than Isfarkand and more versatile than both which isn't a knock on Ormonde Jayne at all.  Could use a little more musk but otherwise really quite complete.  Almost stunning.  It's a shame that the name and bottle are so terribly tacky.  I'll get over it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="2278183"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=2278183#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2271110" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2259683" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Jetpack"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2230006"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2230006.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Jetpack" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2259683ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2259683" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2230006">Jetpack</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-24">08/24/24 12:27</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Toy Boy by Moschino has carved out its niche as a standout rose-pepper fragrance, and it’s clear why it’s so popular. Launched in 2019, this scent mixes spicy pink pepper with a rich rose absolute, creating a unique blend that’s both bold and surprisingly versatile. It's one of those rare fragrances that blurs the lines between masculine and feminine, making it genuinely unisex.<br />
<br />
What sets Toy Boy apart is not just the scent itself but its accessible price point. For a fragrance that delivers such a unique combination of rose and spice, it’s surprisingly affordable. This is likely why it's become so well-loved—and, yes, sometimes hated due to its popularity. But don’t let that stop you. If you’re looking for something different that won't empty your wallet, Toy Boy is worth a try. It’s modern, edgy, and perfect for anyone who wants to make a statement, regardless of gender. Give it a chance, and you might find it’s exactly what you’ve been looking for.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="2259683"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=2259683#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2255923" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; pair with a huge dose of pink pepper. The pepper does not add spiciness so much a sort of 'mouth-watering' savory quality. <br />
<br />
I was very excited to find the little black honey bear out in the wild at my local T.J. Maxx. I took him home and wore the fragrance out on the Fourth of July. Toy Boy has good longevity, especially in the summer heat: it remained virtually unchanged for 2 hours or so.<br />
<br />
Nevertheless, this fragrance is not currently in my rotation. Toy Boy is very linear: it is the same, very green, peppery rose throughout the entire wear. It does not dry down to reveal other facets (at least on me). I started to find it quite cloying after a time. <br />
<br />
I do like the bear, though!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="2252740"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=2252740#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2248217" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
I will agree the opening can be something that can turn you away from this fragrance, what im talking about is the heavy use of elemi that at least my nose picks up, which gives this a sour vibe, relating it to pickles like some people have is a bit extreme though, I literally have a jar of pickles in my mini fridge and no, they dont smell alike.<br />
<br />
The beauty of this fragrance is in the mid and especially the dry down, when the sourness goes away and the rose becomes more present, it becomes a fresh rose, with the sweetness of pear, with woods and and a smooth cashmeran.<br />
<br />
Honestly, spraying this is on clothes is THE move, the best part of the fragrance sticks on clothes for so long and for me personally it performs better than on my skin. You can wear this year round, just go easy on the sprays when its hot outside. Wear this with confidence, and you will smell amazing!<br />
<br />
Affordable, high quality, versatile, and unique. This scent is a stellar signature fragrance. 9.5/10.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="2225327"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=2225327#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2218653" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2037123">Wild_Willy</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-10">07/10/24 20:16</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>One of the most beautiful, elegant men’s fragrances I’ve smelt so far and also one of the longest lasting. This palate of notes for a men’s fragrance is definitely not mass appealing and for any male that doesn’t appreciate and enjoy heavy floral notes in a fragrance you most likely will not enjoy this on yourself. Like others have said you have to be a particular type of male to pull this one off out in the public’s nose path. In my opinion you either have to be slightly feminine or the exact opposite and be totally confident and masculine “Alpha” if you will.. although I don’t like that term. I personally love this fragrance so much as I have always been a huge fan of Rose in men’s fragrances. This fragrance immediately starts out a little rowdy and almost too floral strong but quickly transform into a more deep clean masculine floral as it drys down. I can also say Toy Boy is an absolute longevity, sillage maniac. I work a mostly labor intensive job where I’m sweating regularly and it’s the middle of summer with high heat and humidity currently. I sprayed this twice on each forearm before work and could still smell it on my skin and slightly in the air 8+ hours later. This won’t be for everyone but for the ones who can really appreciate floral heavy men’s fragrances it’s an absolute winner!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="2214727"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=2214727#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2214241" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Settles down quickly enough to a very nice red rose, musks, wood and pink pepper scent. Fruit Scents<br />
<br />
Lovely fragrance</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="2198230"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=2198230#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2196018" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2196018" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="artpopw"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2159622"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2159622.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="artpopw" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2196018ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2196018" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.74); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2159622">artpopw</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-22">06/22/24 07:59</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Amazing peppery and slightly sour rose with spices and florals, which gradually becomes more fruity and creamy, quite unique yet beautiful, and I don't get any of those strange associations like pickles or an old grandma. Can even pick some incense there at the start, on me it opens mainly as a cute rose with a bit of spices and for me it's pretty much unisex. Not a safe blind buy, spices may be too harsh for some people and rose too sour. Really long lasting, I get 3+ hours of noticeable projection and 6+ hours of longevity. I'm not an advanced perfume enthusiast, but I really liked this one, it's definitely worth a try</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="2196018"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=2196018#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2195240" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2195240" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Chiru"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1015703"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1015703.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Chiru" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Noir-Extreme-29675.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.29675.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Noir Extreme"title="Noir Extreme"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2195240ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2195240" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.72); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1015703">Chiru</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-21">06/21/24 11:10</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Lovely. Reviewers had me worried this would be too polarizing, too feminine, too avant garde, too [insert issue here]. Nah, there's nothing scary about Toy Boy at all. Roses come in many different shapes, sizes, and smells. I have tea roses in my garden that similarly resemble this type of rose profile, though obviously Toy Boy isn't as natural. It's a pretty simple scent, really. A dry, earthy rose, with pink pepper, spiced pear, and light citrus. That's all it is. Fairly linear throughout the life of the scent. I'm really enjoying this. <br />
<br />
Whether to pick this up or not is actually a pretty easy decision in my opinion. This is unisex leaning masculine thanks to the pear and pepper. If you're a man who isn't afraid of rose scents, you need this. If you don't like roses, you may not like this, because it's entirely rose dominant. However, take into consideration that even if you don't like rose, this isn't your typical rose perfume. It doesn't really resemble the rose profiles found in most fragrances targeting women, nor does it resemble the rose found in your typical oud rose perfumes for men. You don't need gloves to handle Toy Boy, it's pretty approachable. <br />
<br />
I'm fully aware of my entirely blasé approach towards the flak Toy Boy is getting in these comments; it's certainly not for everyone, but really, some of these reviews are going pretty overboard and I feel are scaring people away from an otherwise really great scent. Yeah, it's not a mass pleasing blue freshie, but it's not Encre Noir or Terroni either. The best advice that can be given with approaching this scent is to sample it first. It's not really blind buy safe, (because it has rose in it) but it's also nothing scary either and I'd recommend people check it out first and not be put off due to some of the comments. <br />
<br />
Performance is amazing. Longevity is everything I want in a fragrance, as it easily does 8+ hours with projection being excellent at 3+ hours. Absolutely no clue what people are talking about with the dill pickle stuff. I don't get any of that. Will be rocking this hard this upcoming fall when the weather cools down. Honestly, as long as you're careful with the sprays, I think it's fine for warm weather as well, though perhaps not in the dead of summer. This will make a fantastic pair with Cartier's Declaration D'Un Soir. Toy Boy is more playful, sexy, and easygoing while D'Un Soir is more polished, professional, and serious. Both share a similar approach on a modern, masculine rose. Recommended.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="2195240"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=2195240#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2193798" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Not office friendly, not extreme heat friendly, btw. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2148100">mosmells</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-03">06/03/24 19:41</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Toy Boy opens up with an intense blend of rose covered with pink pepper and a pear that lingers in the background. The rose takes the show as the fragrance goes on, with the pepper and fruit settling down into this musky background that just creates this beautiful, seductive scent. As the fragrance dries down more, the sandalwood creeps in and adds such a heavy, creamy touch to the fragrance that creates the perfect dry-down. It has beastly performance with a very strong sillage. This thing has gotten me tons of compliments, but it's also the first fragrance someones complained about. While it can be a polarizing scent, Moschino Toy Boy is a masterpiece.<br />
<br />
10/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="2177188"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=2177188#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2172542" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; A bouncy radiant rose dropping petals from a bouquet tucked under an arm. A rose in the center of a table in a clear glass vase beckoning you to bury your nose. Pear is used sparingly and really livens up the rose. Elemi and pepper do a beautiful balancing act to keep it from getting cloying the way ELDO 'Hermann A Mes' does although theyre distant cousins in the 'wet rose' genre. Performance is phenomenal. 7+hrs on skin. Sillage is pretty much a rose petal trail. Dry down is creamy sandalwood with the soft touch of Cashmeran and a thick amber. The most similar fragrance to 'Toy Boy' I've tried is Commes 'Zero' but it's flat and muted for nearly quadruple the price.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="2151142"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=2151142#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2150389" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2024437">paulquality</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-24">04/24/24 19:48</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Unlike any other mens designer frag I have smelled. It's got that spicy, almost hand soap like feel, with a very prominent rose. It's sexy, playful and mysterious with a playboy like charm that will intrigue anyone who smells you. Of course the rose is what makes this so polarizing, but that's what makes it standout. It's rounded off with a touch of sweetness and pepper with some smooth woods, but it's an largely an unapolagetic rose scent. <br />
<br />
This frag wont give you confidence, you need to be that guy already. Seriously, most people dont expect a man to smell like this, and you have to be ready to own it. Longevity, projection and sillage are all incredible for the price. I used to think the bottle was tacky but it actually grew on me alot and stands out in any collection. <br />
<br />
If you want to actually turn heads and leave a real impression, then this should be your next pickup. Signature scent worthy, however those suffering from fragile masculinity will struggle alot with this one.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="2135474"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=2135474#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2134457" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I cant smell it passed 1 hour :/</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="2103065"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=2103065#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2099040" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2099040" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Justin Ninja"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1109520"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1109520.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Justin Ninja" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Maison-Alhambra/Versencia-Essence-93817.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.93817.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Versencia Essence"title="Versencia Essence"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2099040ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2099040" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1109520">Justin Ninja</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-20">03/20/24 21:39</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Let me prefix my review by saying this is one of the greatest rose fragrances for men, and there are few. The fragrance opens with a blast of pear skin, bergamot, and elemi resin, showcasing it's lemon and pepper facets. Pink pepper soon follows, and it's zingy, spicy facets blend perfectly with the heart of rose. I had never encountered a "flax" note in perfume before, which appears alongside the rose. I have encountered linseed oil before in school art class. That is here: it is an oily, slightly nutty aroma. The warm spicy/ woody aroma of cloves and nutmeg soon follow. I am not a fan of this part of the fragrance. The spices distract from the theme of a botanical green rose. I believe this botanical quality is bolstered, in the best way, by the use of Undecavertol, an aroma chemical with pear, cucumber, and violet leaf facets. A distinguished magnolia flower is absent to my nose. However, there is a slight soapy citrus floral note here. The base notes are muted, as rose is the real star here--- a rose that reads mostly masculine, amazingly. The base notes most present to my nose are Cashmeran and Sylkolide: nose piercing, amber/ musk aroma chemicals. They work wonderfully here, as they stay alert and never mellow the radiant rose.<br />
My biggest gripe with the fragrance is the bottle design. I love the black bear. However, the octagon shaped knob on his head is unnecessary, and deceiving. He would have looked much cuter without  that knob. More importantly, though, that sturdy knob implies that the bottle could be lifted by the head. I attempted to do that one night and the entire base crashed to the ground. Now the atomizer is broken and I have to use it as a splash.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="2099040"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=2099040#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2097730" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
This isn't a bad fragance , I think its okay. , but I can see while some people might not , Main notes i get is a soapy rose with that creamy sandalwood base , Definetely a unisex scent , Maybe even leaning more feminine , As a man i would not feel comfortable wearing this although it is a nice fragrance, This could smell like an ''old lady'' to some people . It kind of smells like a bar of rose soap that you would find in your grandparent's bathroom.<br />
<br />
Scent : 6.5/10<br />
<br />
Performance : 7/10 , Its pretty good you're gonna get around 6-7 hours with a decent projection first couple hours<br />
<br />
Price : 7.5/10 , You get pretty good quality of ingredients at a decent price like you can find this for 35-50$<br />
<br />
Overall : 7/10<br />
<br />
As for seasons to wear this , You could pull it off year round but not in either extreme ( No extreme cold or extreme hot ) perfect for like around  15-20 degree C weather ( 59-68 F )</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; But I've kept the hope that I'd find something else I like. Enter Toy Boy! <br />
<br />
I love the bright "green" scent that this perfume has.  I don't get any rose or pepper, but only a wonderful, crisp, clean pear smell that is NOT sugary sweet.  It's got a tiny bit of tartness on me that I actually really enjoy.  <br />
<br />

Do I like it: So-so, it goes too sour on me <br />
Who it is: A vampiric flirt that still holds a grudge against their ex <br />
Smells I get: pepper, sour accord, pink rose<br />

<br />
A big, ol' grown up pink rose with a good dose of pepper on it. Pretty sour, rich, tad spicy. Not sweet.<br />

While I do like smell of pepper, I think it belongs more on food.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="2059657"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=2059657#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2057107" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2057107" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Snydes88"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1964904"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1964904.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Snydes88" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Rabanne/1-Million-Lucky-48903.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.48903.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="1 Million Lucky"title="1 Million Lucky"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2057107ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2057107" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.72); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1964904">Snydes88</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-09">02/09/24 07:24</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Where to begin with this fragrance....I see alot of mixed reviews and I can see why. This is definitely not a blind buy fragrance  because of the strong rose scent.  You gotta love how this DNA smells (Floral/rose). Do you research and test it out at your local fragrance store. Take everyone's review with a grain of salt  including mine. It's all about how your body chemicals reacts to the fragrance and how your reacts.  To me....I Absolutely love this fragrance!! This is a top 10 all time for me!! It's a light spicy and semi sweet fragrance with strong powdery Rose and floral notes. In the base, cashmeran and musky amber are the main players.  For the scent,  I give it a 5/5....very unique fragrance that makes a strong and stunning statement for sure. 👌🏼The second reason I love this fragrance is that fact of it's "Beast Mode" performance. I personally get 9 -11 hours, with 10 hours being average on skin.  12+ hours on clothes,  in fact there has been times where I would smell it days later on clothing.  The projection and sillaged are top notch aswell. 👌🏼This is a 3- 4 spray fragrance. Hours 1 through 3 are beast modes, with projection 5+ feet with an amazing scent trail.  Hours 3 to 6 are border lines beast mode with projection of 3-5 ft with a moderate scent trail. Hours 6 to 9 this fragrance continues to perform which absolutely amazes me. The projection is roughly a arms length (2-3ft) and has light but still noticeable sillaged.  Hours 9 to 11 , I'm still impressed! Projection is about a foot before slowly becoming a skin scent. You get light whiffs from time to time. Over spraying this fragrance can be a devastating for everyone in the room you spray it in. Just be mindful and curious of others.  I rate this performance a 5/5!! I bought this fragrance for $61.73 for a 3.4 once.  You can get the sample and travel sizes for cheap. ( $15.00 and below)  Great deal on testing it out on your skin.  You definitely get a good quality product and is worth the price in my book. I rate this price a 5/5! Overall I rate this fragrance a 5/5, which is rare for me to give a perfect score out...but I feel for the price point, quality, performance and uniqueness  you can't go wrong here. I would wear this for a date night or a night out situation....more so for the second option. Winter, spring and fall works best....but even on a cooler summer night (50°s and 60°s ) could work....just dial the sprays back.  I recommend you getting your nose on this fragrance!!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="2057107"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=2057107#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2056718" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I tried this in Superdrug just over a year ago and I found it to be amazing that the next time I was there I bought it, 50ml. I think I thought it smelled like lacoste blanc however I haven't tried that fragrance in however long. So the sexy teddy bear cap came off and 5 sprays on my neck was blasted; straight away it hit me with that beautiful rose and pink pepper and a nice light musk. Toy Boy is a very unisex fragrance however leans slightly on the masculine side, in the mid aside from the rose I can detect the floral flax and magnolia and spices from the cloves. Deeper into the life of this fragrance hours and hours later the base picks up traction and shines! Toy Boy gets a little warmer from the amber and a little animalic smelling from the sylkolide but also earthier and sexier from the gorgeous Vetiver and Sandalwood. I think this fragrance is so unique and niche smelling for an inexpensive designer fragrance! Moschino have been brave and very bold but it works. Beastmode performance 14+ hours and many compliments guaranteed, just smells so pure and saucy in the cooler weather...oh and the bottle is a perfect 10/10 😜🐻🌹<br />
<br />
Price 8/10<br />
Longevity 10/10<br />
Scent 9.5/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="2051456"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=2051456#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2046518" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1739161">vanillalova</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-01-24">01/24/24 01:45</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>my go to signature scent, my favourite rose scent so far.<br />
Rose is a tricky note for most men, as we acquaint it towards the opposite sex. Moschino was being Creative when they made this. Yes the bottle is a bit tacky, but at least the bottle is heavy and feels high quality, least we forget the fire hose of a pressurised atomiser it has!<br />
<br />
Scent:<br />
The rose in this comes off in more of a rose-water type of way, light and refreshing, not syrupy like say a Turkish delight/Bandung. Pink pepper plays a big part in helping add some spice, with a slight hint of pear for fruity sweetness. Something in the background is pushing off some earthy, dirty tones, which helps pull it ever so slightly towards the masculine side(still unisex overall). Personally, love rose when it's done this way, light and refreshing, instead of a syrup-like-sweetness like Bandung has. Overall very smooth, high quality, and doesn't smell very synthetic. Some say it smells like a funeral, which I gotta somewhat agree with, though I'd recognise this as more of an auntie/grandma scent, loving in a way lol(my aunt literally smells like this). This IS a polarising scent for guys, so if you dislike it, that's fine, and most people will think so too, this reaches far into the side of creativity for men's colognes.<br />
<br />
longevity:<br />
Outstanding, 8h+ on a hot day. It projects more than usual, abt 2ft for I'd say about 2+ hours. It slowly dies into a skin scent only by the 5th hour, which up till then I still catch whiffs of it. I think if you were to spray this on your wrist, it may smell like it it isn't projecting, but it's most likely that you have gone anosmic, as even during the 3rd hour of my wearing, my friend went "You smell like wet roses bro"😭.<br />
Edit: Pissed off a friend who sits next to me for class even though i only wor one spray on my neck.<br />
(2sprays, 31c heat, 1/2 on each elbow one on the back of my neck)<br />
<br />
when to wear?<br />
I myself wear it to work/school, but I'd suggest it more for outings.<br />
apply liberally on hotter days(max 2), not sure what age group this fits though.<br />
at the end of the day wear what you want!<br />
<br />
TLDR<br />
none cause I'm lazy :P</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="2040264"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=2040264#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2038649" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It’s very centered around the rose and a fresh, spicy opening. Unsurprisingly my girlfriend and other people I talked to don’t like it lol. Performance is great.<br />
It’s also not to my personal taste, but sometimes I am in the mood for it, and the quality of this is undeniable.<br />
I see the comparison you could draw to Hermann à mes Côtés me Paraissait une Ombre but I feel like this is more abrasive and louder, while Hermann (…) is softer, more introverted and less spicy.<br />
It’s not my personal cup of tea, but you can’t really argue with the creativity, longevity and price of this.<br />
It may not be a safe blind buy, but for 20 bucks a 30ml isn’t expensive and is gonna last you a long time.<br />
Atomizer is good.<br />
<br />
Scent: 7/10<br />
Projection: 8/10<br />
Longevity: 9/10<br />
Versatility: 6/10<br />
Price: 9/10<br />
<br />
Overall: 7,8/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="2026203"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=2026203#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2025466" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Blind buy. Can’t say I’m disappointed but not impressed either. Literally roses with a hint of musk. Take the musk away and it’s literally a feminine fragrance. I can see it easily being a female appealer as it is floral and delicate yet the musk adds some masculinity to it, kind of like a preppy floral boy. For an eau de parfum, I wasn’t expecting this based on the reviews I read here, but surprisingly, for me, it falls short regarding its longevity and its sillage, at least on my skin, maybe because the smell is somewhat more delicate and gentle. 30 mins in and almost all of the smell is already gone. Definitely lasts longer on clothing. I have eau de toilettes that last longer. 6.5 out of 10. Safe fragrance for a chill, cold night out with a first date. Can definitely see myself wearing this more at night. Summer and winter friendly, leaning more towards winter.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="2020473"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=2020473#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2020154" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;                             <div id="parent1404653" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1404653" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Lamont Cranston"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1220703"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1220703.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Lamont Cranston" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Armani-Code-Absolu-53106.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.53106.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Armani Code Absolu"title="Armani Code Absolu"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1404653ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck9x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1404653" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1220703">Lamont Cranston</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-09-04">09/04/21 23:04</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A word of warning: this is NOT a safe blind buy. Even if you like the smell of rose, you haven't smelled anything like this. I have to give the perfumer credit for creating a brilliant, complex, unique scent like Toy Boy in a world drowning in "Blue" fragrances. However, I must admit that I intensely dislike it. Do not let my dislike dissuade you from sampling this if the Fragrantica note breakdown (which is very accurate for Toy Boy) appeals to you.<br />
<br />
It opens with VERY heavy rose and pepper. Now, maybe you're thinking to yourself "I've smelled rose scented fragrances before." Um no. There are rose scented fragrances...and then there's Toy Boy. Imagine you're lounging on a bed of rose petals wearing pajamas made of rose petals while eating a rose petal salad and the song playing on the radio is "Every Rose has Its Thorn." Then you'll be in the vicinity of the ballpark of Toy Boy. <br />
<br />
Rose is still prominently at the wheel during the drydown but bergamot is also a backseat passenger. The base is still more rose with some flashes of cashmere and sandalwood. <br />
<br />
The longevity and sillage of Toy Boy are off the charts. Handle with care. Four sprays and you will choke out a room for hours. There are some fragrances out there that I hate and I just can't see how anyone enjoys them. This is not the case with Toy Boy. I can completely understand how someone could love this and make it their signature scent.<br />
<br />
Once again, I applaud the perfumer for creating such a rose heavy scent that is still unmistakably masculine and for crafting such a unique, outside-the-box fragrance. We need more mainstream, yet still avant garde, releases like Toy Boy.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="1404653"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=1404653#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1534012" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; You will pull a lot of attention wearing this one. Because people will try to find out who smells so bad. And trust me they will find you like they did me. To this day im still traumatized. I wake up almost every night from the nightmare that was the curse of me spraying this perfume on myself. <br />
Once again, let me warn you. This is polarizing smell I people do not like it. Except if you live in drakula style mansion than this is just the fragrance for you.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="1534012"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=1534012#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1122080" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/112173">ricorto</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2019-12-06">12/06/19 05:46</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I am wearing it for two weeks. Blind buy. I still don't know how to describe TOY BOY.<br />
It is a sweet woody rose pungent fragrance. Enormous sillage and projection. <br />
I don't think it's a crowd-pleaser but it is unique.<br />
<br />
After a few weeks, I have to say... I hate it. Repulsive frag, so strong and annoying. I can´t help, but it smells like manure and roses, to me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="55858"comment_id="1122080"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Moschino/Toy-Boy-55858.html?ccid=1122080#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1165018" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1100485">Deutsch100</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-04-17">04/17/20 22:17</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>My bottle of Toy Boy arrived today from Selfridge's in London.  Really cool bottle, and the black prevents it from looking too "cute" :)<br />
I really like it, but don't love it yet.  One of my most dreaded scents in the world is Shaghaf Oud, and this smells like a combo of that mixed with Tom Ford Rose Prick (which I love).<br />
<br />
The floral rose note in Toy Boy is awesome, bridging masculine and feminine (my fav). There must be some oud or saffron in Toy Boy and this is what reminds me so much of Shaghaf Oud.<br />
<br />
So often we complain about, and for good reason, that many new fragrances do not last or project enough.  Well, for once I wished Toy Boy did not last as long, nor project as far, LOL. O N E spray on my wrist is going near full strength for almost 5 hours.  Sounds good, yeah? I don't enjoy constantly smelling what I am wearing non-stop. It is almost cloying, I can almost taste it, it lasts so long and is so strong!<br />
<br />
I will keep trying Toy Boy, as it seems very well made and a great value, but you must really like it, because you and everyone around you will smell it all day or night ;)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex;
